reason for deferral.\n   482→// Reasons like instance count unknown and deferred prereq are not\n   483→// relevant for providers but can occur in general.\n   484→type DeferredReason string\n   485→\n   486→const (\n   487→\t// DeferredReasonInvalid is used when the reason for deferring is\n   488→\t// unknown or irrelevant.\n   489→\tDeferredReasonInvalid DeferredReason = \"invalid\"\n   490→\n   491→\t// DeferredReasonInstanceCountUnknown is used when the reason for deferring\n   492→\t// is that the count or for_each meta-attribute was unknown.\n   493→\tDeferredReasonInstanceCountUnknown DeferredReason = \"instance_count_unknown\"\n   494→\n   495→\t// DeferredReasonResourceConfigUnknown is used when the reason for deferring\n   496→\t// is
